Addresses deep-review finding M-001.\"\n4: ---\n5: \n6: # Rename Pattern — mechanical refactor template\n7: \n8: For any rename refactor that touches multiple surfaces (skill dir, agent files, sibling references, root docs, memory, compiled indexes), follow this pattern. First fully proven in `114-small-ai-model-optimization/007-rename-sk-ai-small-model/` (2026-05-21).\n9: \n10: ---\n11: \n12: ## 1. SURFACE TAXONOMY\n13: \n14: Every rename touches some subset of these categories. Map each before starting.\n15: \n16: | Category | Examples | How to handle |\n17: |---|---|---|\n18: | **The thing being renamed** | `.opencode/skills/<old>/` dir or `.opencode/agents/<old>.md` | `git mv` (preserves history) |\n19: | **Live cross-references** | Sibling skill `graph-metadata.json` `enhances`/`related_to`, command files, manual playbooks | Literal substitution |\n20: | **Live runtime mirrors** | `.claude/agents/`, `.codex/agents/`, `.gemini/agents/` + corresponding READMEs | `git mv` + literal substitution |\n21: | **Live root behavioral docs** | `AGENTS.md`, `CLAUDE.md` (often symlinked), `README.md` | Literal substitution |\n22: | **Live auto-memory** | `~/.claude/projects/.../memory/MEMORY.md` index + current-state memory files | Literal substitution; preserve filename slugs to avoid breaking inbound `[[wikilinks]]` |\n23: | **Live compiled indexes** | `skill-graph.json`, SQLite caches | REGENERATE (never hand-edit) |\n24: | **Historical narrative** | Memory feedback entries describing past incidents under the old name | Tag inline: `(renamed <new> YYYY-MM-DD)` — keep dates intact |\n25: | **Historical spec docs** | Originating packet's `spec.md`/`plan.md`/`tasks.md`/`checklist.md`/`implementation-summary.md` | PRESERVE — do not edit |\n26: | **Historical research/review iterations** | Deep-research / deep-review `iterations/*.md`, `deltas/*.jsonl` | PRESERVE — do not edit |\n27: | **Historical version notes** | Renamed skill's prior `changelog/v*.md` | PRESERVE — add a NEW `vN+1.0.0.md` as forward-link |\n28: | **Frozen bench fixtures** | `benchmarks/.../per-probe.jsonl` recording prior-name state | PRESERVE |\n29: \n30: **Rule of thumb**: If the surface describes work as it happened in the past, preserve. If the surface describes what is true NOW, update.\n31: \n32: ---\n33: \n34: ## 2. WORKFLOW\n35: \n36: ### Phase A — Pre-flight (sequential)\n37: 1. Capture a rg baseline: `rg -l \"<old-name>\" --hidden -g '!node_modules' -g '!.git/**' -g '!**/skill-graph*.sqlite*' > scratch/rg/rg-baseline-before-files.txt`\n38: 2. Classify every hit into live vs historical using the surface taxonomy above. Write `scratch/resource-map.md` + `scratch/rename-plan.json` (the contract — disjoint phase scopes).\n39: 3. Read the cli-X SKILL.md file before composing any cli-X dispatch (per AGENTS.md CLI dispatch rule).\n40: \n41: ### Phase B — Optional cli-devin SWE-1.6 verification\n42: Dispatch 2-4 parallel SWE-1.6 jobs (read-only) to verify the rename plan against each surface group. Each job follows cli-devin/SKILL.md contract (RCAF, medium pre-planning, bundle-gate \"standard\"). Apply bundle gate per [[feedback_cli_devin_bundle_verification]] + [[feedback_bundle_gate_smoke_run]]. Aggregate verified bundles.\n43: \n44: ### Phase C — Execute renames (parallel-eligible across disjoint surface groups)\n45: 1. `git mv` dir/file renames (preserves rename history; `git log --follow` traces back).\n46: 2. Bulk literal substitution via `sed -i ''` (macOS) on the in-scope file list. Use `find -exec` for atomicity across many files.\n47: 3. Special-case the historical-narrative file with surgical edits (insert `(renamed <new> YYYY-MM-DD)` tag rather than rewriting).\n48: 4. Memory files: filename slugs are sticky (preserve `[[wikilinks]]`); only edit body content.\n49: \n50: ### Phase D — Reindex\n51: 1. Regenerate compiled `.opencode/skills/system-skill-advisor/mcp_server/scripts/skill-graph.json` via `python3 skill_graph_compiler.py --export-json --pretty` (per [[feedback_skill_graph_compiler_rebuild]]).\n52: 2. If the compiler hits a pre-existing blocker (wrong category, asymmetric sibling, etc.), fix it incidentally — document as out-of-scope-but-on-critical-path.\n53: 3. Run `advisor_recommend` MCP smoke on a canonical prompt for the renamed thing; expect new name in top-3 confidence ≥ 0.7.\n54: \n55: ### Phase E — Validate\n56: 1. Post-edit `rg \"<old-name>\"` on the live-surface allow-list → expect 0 hits.\n57: 2. Post-edit `rg \"<old-name>\"` on the historical-surface allow-list → expect SAME count as baseline-before (provenance preserved).\n58: 3. `bash validate.sh --strict <spec-folder>` → exit 0.\n59: 4. Reconcile parent metadata via `generate-context.js` (refreshes `children_ids` + `derived.last_active_child_id`).\n60: \n61: ---\n62: \n63: ## 3. CASE-SENSITIVITY GOTCHA\n64: \n65: Per [[feedback_rename_grep_case_insensitive]]: the final-gate grep MUST use `rg -il` (case-insensitive). UPPERCASE / Title-Case / underscore variants are easy to miss. Always also check for the underscore variant of any hyphenated identifier (e.g., `sk_small_model` next to `sk-small-model`) — Python pseudocode in SKILL.md examples often uses underscores.\n66: \n67: ---\n68: \n69: ## 4. BRANCH POLICY\n70: \n71: Per [[feedback_stay_on_main_no_feature_branches]] — stay on `main`. `create.sh` auto-branches; switch back to `main` and delete the auto-created branch (carry uncommitted changes; cherry-pick any orphan continuity commits first).\n72: \n73: Rename refactors are reversible via `git revert` since `git mv` history is preserved. No need to feature-branch.\n74: \n75: ---\n76: \n77: ## 5. PER-PHASE-CHILD SCOPE DISCIPLINE\n78: \n79: When the rename arc is a phase-parent with multiple children:\n80: - Each phase child's `spec.md` §3 In Scope + Out of Scope is the conflict-prevention contract.\n81: - The rename-plan.json from preflight enforces disjoint file scopes across phase children.\n82: - Phases that touch disjoint file sets can be executed in parallel by separate operators.\n83: \n84: ---\n85: \n86: ## 6. ANTI-PATTERNS TO AVOID\n87: \n88: | Anti-pattern | Why it's wrong | Do this instead |\n89: |---|---|---|\n90: | Hand-editing compiled `skill-graph.json` | Compiled artifact gets overwritten next compile | Regenerate via `skill_graph_compiler.py` |\n91: | Renaming auto-memory file slugs | Breaks inbound `[[wikilinks]]` in MEMORY.md and other memory files | Preserve slug; edit body content only |\n92: | Rewriting historical narrative to use new name | Falsifies past-tense provenance | Insert `(renamed <new> YYYY-MM-DD)` tag |\n93: | Editing the renamed skill's own `changelog/v1+v2*.md` | Historical version state | Add NEW `vN+1.0.0.md` as forward-link |\n94: | Creating a feature branch | Out of policy ([[feedback_stay_on_main_no_feature_branches]]) | Stay on `main`; `git revert` is the rollback path |\n95: | Forgetting case variants | Misses `sk_small_model` (underscore), `Sk-Small-Model` (title), `SK-SMALL-MODEL` (banner) | Use `rg -il` and dedicated 2nd sed pass for underscore identifiers |\n96: \n97: ---\n98: \n99: ## 7. WORKED EXAMPLE — 114/007\n100: \n101: See `.opencode/specs/skilled-agent-orchestration/114-small-ai-model-optimization/007-rename-sk-ai-small-model/` for the full applied pattern:\n102: - spec.md §3 In Scope / Out of Scope is the model classifier\n103: - plan.md §4 IMPLEMENTATION PHASES (A through G) is the workflow timeline\n104: - implementation-summary.md §What Was Built lists the actual surface counts (22 live files, 5 dir/file renames, 1 new changelog)\n105: - review-report.md (deep-review 9-iter PASS+advisories) verifies the pattern's correctness\n106: \n107: ---\n108: \n109: ## 8. CHECKLIST (copy into spec packet)\n110: \n111: - [ ] rg baseline captured to `scratch/rg/rg-baseline-before-files.txt`\n112: - [ ] Per-file live/historical classification written to `scratch/resource-map.md`\n113: - [ ] Disjoint phase scopes in `scratch/rename-plan.json` (jq intersection check = empty)\n114: - [ ] cli-X SKILL.md read before composing any cli-X dispatch\n115: - [ ] All `git mv` renames execute cleanly\n116: - [ ] `sed -i ''` bulk pass (hyphenated form)\n117: - [ ] Second sed pass for underscore variants (where applicable)\n118: - [ ] Auto-memory filename slugs preserved; only body content edited\n119: - [ ] Historical-narrative files tagged inline, not rewritten\n120: - [ ] New `vN+1.0.0.md` changelog created on the renamed skill\n121: - [ ] Compiled `skill-graph.json` regenerated via `skill_graph_compiler.py`\n122: - [ ] `advisor_recommend` smoke confirms new name surfaces ≥ 0.7\n123: - [ ] Live-surface rg returns 0 hits\n124: - [ ] Historical-surface rg returns SAME count as baseline-before\n125: - [ ] `validate.sh --strict <spec-folder>` exit 0\n126: - [ ] Parent metadata reconciled via `generate-context.js`\n127: - [ ] Packet-local changelog generated via `nested-changelog.js`\n128: - [ ] `git log --follow` traces renamed file back to original\n\n(End of file - total 128 lines)\n</content>","metadata":{"preview":"---\ntitle: \"Rename Pattern — mechanical refactor template for skill/agent identity changes\"\ndescription: \"Reusable pattern + checklist for repo-wide rename refactors.
